Alerting Engine\\n\\nThe legacy alerting engine in Grafana is defined in **pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go**, which creates and manages the following database tables:\\n\\n1. **alert** - The core legacy alert table containing dashboard-based alerts with fields like dashboard_id, panel_id, name, message, state, settings, frequency, handler, severity, silenced, execution_error, eval_data, eval_date, new_state_date, state_changes, created, and updated.\\n\\n2. **alert_notification** - Stores legacy alert notification channels (name, type, settings)\\n\\n3. **alert_rule_tag** - Tags associated with legacy alert rules\\n\\nThese tables represent the pre-8.0 alert system in Grafana that was dashboard-centric and tied to specific dashboard panels.\\n\\n### Unified Alerting (ngalert) Storage\\n\\nThe unified alerting engine is implemented across multiple locations:\\n\\n#### Core Storage Implementation\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go** (DBstore): Main implementation of the RuleStore interface providing methods like GetAlertRuleByUID, ListAlertRules, ListAlertRulesPaginated, InsertAlertRules, UpdateAlertRules, DeleteAlertRulesByUID, and state management.\\n\\n- **pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go**: Defines all unified alerting tables including:\\n  - alert_rule: Stores alert rule definitions with UID, OrgID, title, condition, data, labels, annotations, namespace_uid, rule_group, eval_behavior, etc.\\n  - alert_rule_version: Tracks version history of alert rules\\n  - alert_definition: Stores alert definitions\\n  - alert_definition_version: Version tracking for definitions\\n  - alert_instance: Tracks current alert instances/states\\n  - alert_rule_state: Stores rule state history\\n  - alert_configuration: Stores alertmanager configurations\\n  - alert_configuration_history: Tracks configuration versions\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/store/alertmanager.go**: Handles alertmanager-specific storage\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go**: Defines the AlertRule, AlertRuleKey, and related model types used throughout the unified alerting system\\n\\n#### Legacy Storage Wrappers for Backward Compatibility\\n\\nThe system maintains backward compatibility through legacy storage implementations:\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/config.go**: Stores and manages alertmanager configurations for backward compatibility\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/compat.go**: Contains conversion functions like InhibitRuleToInhibitionRule for converting legacy format to unified format\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/imported.go**: Handles imported legacy configurations (especially from Prometheus/external sources) with the ImportedConfigRevision structure managing merged rules, routes, and receivers\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/routes.go**: Manages legacy routing tree definitions\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/receivers.go**: Handles legacy receiver (notification channel) definitions\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/inhibition_rules.go**: Manages inhibition rules with backward compatibility\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/persist.go**: Defines storage interface for persisting legacy alertmanager configs\\n\\n#### Registry Apps Storage Layers\\n\\n- **pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/legacy_storage.go**: Provides legacy storage wrapper for alert rules (type legacyStorage)\\n\\n- **pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/legacy_storage.go**: Provides legacy storage wrapper for recording rules\\n\\n- **pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/receiver/legacy_storage.go**: Legacy storage for notification receivers\\n\\n- **pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/routingtree/legacy_storage.go**: Legacy storage for routing trees\\n\\n### Migration and Conversion Scripts\\n\\n#### Main Migration Engine\\n\\n**pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go**: The core migration that executes the upgrade from legacy alerting to unified alerting. The upgradeNgAlerting type implements CodeMigration interface and:\\n\\n1. Updates alert configurations from legacy format\\n2. Migrates alertmanager configuration files\\n3. Handles organization assignment for configurations\\n4. Includes FixEarlyMigration for handling configurations created before version 8.2 with org_id=0\\n\\n**pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go**: Defines all database table migrations for the unified alerting system, including the AddTablesMigrations function that sets up alert_rule, alert_rule_version, and related tables.\\n\\n#### Prometheus/Alertmanager Conversion\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_convert_prometheus.go**: Implements ConvertPrometheusSrv service for converting Prometheus-compatible alerting rules to Grafana format:\\n\\n1. **RouteConvertPrometheusGetRules**: Returns all Grafana-managed alert rules imported from Prometheus sources\\n2. **RouteConvertPrometheusGetAlertmanagerConfig**: Retrieves imported Alertmanager configurations\\n3. **NewConvertPrometheusSrv**: Initializes the conversion service with rule store, datasource cache, and alert rule service\\n\\nThis service enables importing rules from Mimir and other Prometheus-compatible systems while preserving the original rule definitions for round-trip compatibility.\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/api/prometheus_conversion.go**: Handler wrapper for the conversion API endpoints\\n\\n#### Compatibility Layer\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/store/compat.go**: Provides compatibility functions for converting between legacy and new formats:\\n- convertAlertRuleToModel: Converts alertRule database objects to ngalert models.AlertRule\\n- AlertRuleConvertOptions: Controls which fields to parse during conversion\\n\\n#### Provisioning API\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/alert_rules.go**: Implements AlertRuleService for rule provisioning:\\n- Manages rule CRUD operations\\n- Handles rule group operations\\n- Manages provenance (who created/modified rules)\\n- Enforces access control\\n- Validates rule groups and quotas\\n- Integrates with folder service for namespace management\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_provisioning.go**: Provisioning API implementation using AlertRuleService\\n\\n### Migration Flow\\n\\nThe migration path from legacy to unified alerting:\\n\\n1. **Legacy System** (dashboard alerts in alert table)\\n   ↓\\n2. **Migration Code** (upgradeNgAlerting migration)\\n   ↓\\n3. **Unified Storage** (alert_rule table and related tables)\\n   ↓\\n4. **Provisioning API** (AlertRuleService)\\n   ↓\\n5. **Conversion API** (ConvertPrometheusSrv for Prometheus imports)\\n\\nThe legacy storage wrapper classes maintain backward compatibility by wrapping the unified storage while converting between legacy and new formats on-the-fly, allowing existing code and external tools (like mimirtool) to continue working with the implementation of the RuleStore interface providing methods like GetAlertRuleByUID, ListAlertRules, ListAlertRulesPaginated, InsertAlertRules, UpdateAlertRules, DeleteAlertRulesByUID, and state management.\\n\\n- **pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go**: Defines all unified alerting tables including:\\n  - alert_rule: Stores alert rule definitions with UID, OrgID, title, condition, data, labels, annotations, namespace_uid, rule_group, eval_behavior, etc.\\n  - alert_rule_version: Tracks version history of alert rules\\n  - alert_definition: Stores alert definitions\\n  - alert_definition_version: Version tracking for definitions\\n  - alert_instance: Tracks current alert instances/states\\n  - alert_rule_state: Stores rule state history\\n  - alert_configuration: Stores alertmanager configurations\\n  - alert_configuration_history: Tracks configuration versions\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/store/alertmanager.go**: Handles alertmanager-specific storage\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go**: Defines the AlertRule, AlertRuleKey, and related model types used throughout the unified alerting system\\n\\n#### Legacy Storage Wrappers for Backward Compatibility\\n\\nThe system maintains backward compatibility through legacy storage implementations:\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/config.go**: Stores and manages alertmanager configurations for backward compatibility\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/compat.go**: Contains conversion functions like InhibitRuleToInhibitionRule for converting legacy format to unified format\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/imported.go**: Handles imported legacy configurations (especially from Prometheus/external sources) with the ImportedConfigRevision structure managing merged rules, routes, and receivers\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/routes.go**: Manages legacy routing tree definitions\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/receivers.go**: Handles legacy receiver (notification channel) definitions\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/inhibition_rules.go**: **pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/legacy_storage.go**: Provides legacy storage wrapper for recording rules\\n\\n- **pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/receiver/legacy_storage.go**: Legacy storage for notification receivers\\n\\n- **pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/routingtree/legacy_storage.go**: Legacy storage for routing trees\\n\\n### Migration and Conversion Scripts\\n\\n#### Main Migration Engine\\n\\n**pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go**: The core migration that executes the upgrade from legacy alerting to unified alerting. The upgradeNgAlerting type implements CodeMigration interface and:\\n\\n1. Updates alert configurations from legacy format\\n2. Migrates alertmanager configuration files\\n3. Handles organization assignment for configurations\\n4. Includes FixEarlyMigration for handling configurations created before version 8.2 with org_id=0\\n\\n**pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go**: Defines all database table migrations for configurations\\n3. **NewConvertPrometheusSrv**: Initializes the conversion service with rule store, datasource cache, and alert rule service\\n\\nThis service enables importing rules from Mimir and other Prometheus-compatible systems while preserving the original rule definitions for round-trip compatibility.\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/api/prometheus_conversion.go**: Handler wrapper for the API\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/alert_rules.go**: Implements AlertRuleService for rule provisioning:\\n- Manages rule CRUD operations\\n- Handles rule group operations\\n- Manages provenance (who created/modified rules)\\n- Enforces access control\\n- Validates rule groups and quotas\\n- Integrates with folder service for namespace management\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_provisioning.go**: Provisioning API implementation using AlertRuleService\\n\\n### Migration Flow\\n\\nThe migration path from legacy to unified alerting:\\n\\n1. **Legacy System** (dashboard alerts in alert table)\\n   ↓\\n2. **Migration Code** (upgradeNgAlerting migration)\\n   ↓\\n3. **Unified Storage** (alert_rule table and related tables)\\n   ↓\\n4. **Provisioning API** (AlertRuleService)\\n   ↓\\n5. **Conversion API** (ConvertPrometheusSrv for Prometheus imports)\\n\\nThe legacy storage wrapper classes maintain backward compatibility by wrapping the unified storage while converting between legacy and new formats on-the-fly, allowing existing code and external tools (like mimirtool) to continue working with the
